NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
FORM No. 151
[See Rule 315]
Member’s Voluntary Winding up
[Notice of Appointment of Liquidator Pursuant to Section 516 of the Companies Act, 1956.]
Name of Company

:

M/s Sleeves India Automotive Private Limited

Nature of Business

:

Trading in Automobile and Tractor Parts

Address of Registered Office

:

Door No: 12A, Kuppusamy Road, Poothapedu, Chennai-600 089.

Name and Address of Liquidator

:

Mr. V.B.R. Menon
Door No: 12.A, Kuppuswamy Road, Poothapedu, Chennai-600 089.

Date of Appointment

:

06-08-2014

By whom appointed

:

Members

Chennai,
8th August 2014.

V.B.R. MENON,
Liquidator.

SLEEVES INDIA AUTOMOTIVE PVT. LTD.
No. 12-A, Kuppusamy Road, Poothapedu, Ramapuram, Chennai-600 089.
Notice is hereby given for general information that the members of the Sleeves India Automotive Private Limited, at
an Extraordinary General Meeting of the Company held on 6th August, 2014 at 11.30 a.m. at the registered office of the
company at Door No: 12A, Kuppusamy Road, Poothapedu, Chennai-600 089, have passed the following Special Resolution
to wind-up the above Company voluntarily.
Resolved that having regard to the declaration made by the Board of Directors dated the 15th July, 2014 and delivered
to the Registrar of Companies under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company has no debts, the
Company having registered office at Door No: 12A, Kuppusamy Road, Poothapedu, Chennai-600 089, be wound up
voluntarily, pursuant to Section 484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956.
Resolved Further that Mr. V.B.R. Menon, Director having office at 12A, Kuppuswamy Road, Poothapedu, Chennai-600
089, be and is hereby appointed as a Liquidator of the Company pursuant to the provisions of Section 490 of the Companies
Act, 1956, at a remuneration of Rs. 18,000/- (Rupees Eighteen Thousand only) in addition to his costs, charges and
expenses.
(By Order of the Board.)
Chennai,
8th August 2014.

V.B.R. MENON,
Director.

LAKSHMI ENGINE COMPONENTS (INDIA) PRIVATE LIMITED
Regd. Office: Door No. 4B, Survey No. 415, Kunrathur High Road, Kovoor, Kancheepuram-602 101.
Notice is hereby given for general information that the members of the Lakshmi Engine Components (India) Private
Limited, at an Extraordinary General Meeting of the Company held on 6th August, 2014 at 9.30 a.m. at the registered office
of the company at Door No. 4B, Survey No. 415, Kunrathur High Road, Kovoor, Kancheepuram-602 101 have passed the
following Special Resolution to wind-up the above Company voluntarily.
Resolved that having regard to the declaration made by the Board of Directors dated the 15th July, 2014 and delivered
to the Registrar of Companies under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company has no debts, the
Company having registered office at Door No. 4B, Survey No. 415, Kunrathur High Road, Kovoor, Kancheepuram-602 101,
be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to Section 484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956.
Resolved Further that Mr. V.B.R. Menon, Director having office at 12A, Kuppuswamy Road, Poothapedu, Chennai600 089, be and is hereby appointed as a Liquidator of the Company pursuant to the provisions of Section 490 of the
Companies Act, 1956, at a remuneration of Rs. 18,000/- (Rupees Eighteen Thousand only) in addition to his costs, charges
and expenses”.
(By Order of the Board.)

Chennai,
8th August 2014.

V.B.R. MENON,
Director.
